  - blockers: no_actual_setup_level_extracted

- `data_only` data\research\mancini\methodology.txt:74
  - context: My Trade Methodology - Fundamentals | pub=None | plan=None | mode=methodology_definition
  - source_label: methodology_definition
  - levels: setup=none; swept/lost=none; recovered=none; +5=none; invalidation=none; target=none; source_times=none

  - source: Institutions have a set bag of tricks they use to enter the market, and the failed breakdown is #1 on that list.
